# Incident I00201: Fact check: False quotes attributed to Nancy Pelosi, Joe Biden and Alexandria Ocasio-Cortez  

* **Summary:** <i>Social media users have been sharing images online that attribute various quotes to Speaker of the House Nancy Pelosi, Democratic presidential candidate Joe Biden and Rep. Alexandria Ocasio-Cortez. Reuters could not find evidence that these any of these quotes are accurate. </i>

* **incident type**: 

* **Year started:** 

* **Countries:**  , 

* **Found via:** 

* **Date added:** 


| Reference | Pub Date | Authors | Org | Archive |
| --------- | -------- | ------- | --- | ------- |
| [https://www.reuters.com/article/world/fact-checkfalse-quotes-attributed-tonancy-pelosi-joe-biden-and-alexandria-oc-idUSKBN23G26O/](https://www.reuters.com/article/world/fact-checkfalse-quotes-attributed-tonancy-pelosi-joe-biden-and-alexandria-oc-idUSKBN23G26O/) | 2020-06-09 00:00:00 | Reuters | Reuters | [https://archive.is/ecO6p](https://archive.is/ecO6p) |

 

| Technique | Description given for this incident |
| --------- | ------------------------- |
| [T0039.001 Collaborating Assets Seed and Ping](../../generated_pages/techniques/T0039.001.md) | <i>Social media users have been sharing images online that attribute various quotes to Speaker of the House Nancy Pelosi, Democratic presidential candidate Joe Biden and Rep. Alexandria Ocasio-Cortez. Reuters could not find evidence that these any of these quotes are accurate (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution).<br><br>[...]<br><br>The image reads: “’You need to vote for the Democrats, otherwise the illegal aliens will lose their rights.’ – Nancy Pelosi (2019), ‘No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights.’ – Joe Biden, And my personal favorite: ‘Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the Constitution.’ – Alexandria Ocasio Cortez (2018)”<br><br>The image doesn’t say where or when any of the alleged comments were made.<br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters could not find any records of Speaker Pelosi saying “’You need to vote for the Democrats, otherwise the illegal aliens will lose their rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)”<br><br>A Google search brings up pages using this quote with no attribution to a source.<br><br>In a press conference in June 2018, Pelosi told a reporter that using terminology like “illegal alien” is not constructive. The video is available on C-SPAN. Her exact words can be heard around the 15:30 mark. It is therefore unlikely that Pelosi would have used the terminology in the alleged quote. <br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters found no evidence former Vice President Biden ever said the words “No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)” <br><br>Some forums and posts featuring the article link to a Breitbart article that reads, “Biden: No Ordinary American Cares About Their Constitutional Rights, Facebook Questions are Plants”. The article mentions a February 21, 2013 forum at Western Connecticut State University in Danbury where then Vice President Biden spoke about gun control.<br><br>A video on the New York Times website shows Biden’s speech at the university. The closest to the quote in the claim can be seen round the 11:10 mark: “No law-abiding citizen in the United States of America has any fear that their constitutional rights will be infringed in any way. None, zero.”<br><br>The actual quote is significantly different to the quote in this claim. Biden did not say “No ordinary American cares about their constitutional rights”. (T0162: Reframe Context, T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)<br><br>[...]<br><br>“Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the constitution.”<br><br>Reuters could not find any record of Ocasio-Cortez saying this. The social media posts do not provide any context or other information about the purported quote (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution). <br><br>Ocasio-Cortez clarified her stance on the second amendment on the right to keep and bear arms while answering questions on a Reddit thread when she was running as a candidate for Congress in 2017: <br><br>“Combating domestic terrorism? Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |
| [T0039.002 Solicit Production of Fact Check](../../generated_pages/techniques/T0039.002.md) | <i>Social media users have been sharing images online that attribute various quotes to Speaker of the House Nancy Pelosi, Democratic presidential candidate Joe Biden and Rep. Alexandria Ocasio-Cortez. Reuters could not find evidence that these any of these quotes are accurate (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution).<br><br>[...]<br><br>The image reads: “’You need to vote for the Democrats, otherwise the illegal aliens will lose their rights.’ – Nancy Pelosi (2019), ‘No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights.’ – Joe Biden, And my personal favorite: ‘Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the Constitution.’ – Alexandria Ocasio Cortez (2018)”<br><br>The image doesn’t say where or when any of the alleged comments were made.<br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters could not find any records of Speaker Pelosi saying “’You need to vote for the Democrats, otherwise the illegal aliens will lose their rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)”<br><br>A Google search brings up pages using this quote with no attribution to a source.<br><br>In a press conference in June 2018, Pelosi told a reporter that using terminology like “illegal alien” is not constructive. The video is available on C-SPAN. Her exact words can be heard around the 15:30 mark. It is therefore unlikely that Pelosi would have used the terminology in the alleged quote. <br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters found no evidence former Vice President Biden ever said the words “No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)” <br><br>Some forums and posts featuring the article link to a Breitbart article that reads, “Biden: No Ordinary American Cares About Their Constitutional Rights, Facebook Questions are Plants”. The article mentions a February 21, 2013 forum at Western Connecticut State University in Danbury where then Vice President Biden spoke about gun control.<br><br>A video on the New York Times website shows Biden’s speech at the university. The closest to the quote in the claim can be seen round the 11:10 mark: “No law-abiding citizen in the United States of America has any fear that their constitutional rights will be infringed in any way. None, zero.”<br><br>The actual quote is significantly different to the quote in this claim. Biden did not say “No ordinary American cares about their constitutional rights”. (T0162: Reframe Context, T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)<br><br>[...]<br><br>“Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the constitution.”<br><br>Reuters could not find any record of Ocasio-Cortez saying this. The social media posts do not provide any context or other information about the purported quote (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution). <br><br>Ocasio-Cortez clarified her stance on the second amendment on the right to keep and bear arms while answering questions on a Reddit thread when she was running as a candidate for Congress in 2017: <br><br>“Combating domestic terrorism? Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |
| [T0048.005 Voyeuristic Content](../../generated_pages/techniques/T0048.005.md) | <i>Social media users have been sharing images online that attribute various quotes to Speaker of the House Nancy Pelosi, Democratic presidential candidate Joe Biden and Rep. The video is available on C-SPAN. Her exact words can be heard around the 15:30 mark. It is therefore unlikely that Pelosi would have used the terminology in the alleged quote. <br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters found no evidence former Vice President Biden ever said the words “No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)” <br><br>Some forums and posts featuring the article link to a Breitbart article that reads, “Biden: No Ordinary American Cares About Their Constitutional Rights, Facebook Questions are Plants”. If it were a right, it would be in the constitution.”<br><br>Reuters could not find any record of Ocasio-Cortez saying this. The social media posts do not provide any context or other information about the purported quote (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution). <br><br>Ocasio-Cortez clarified her stance on the second amendment on the right to keep and bear arms while answering questions on a Reddit thread when she was running as a candidate for Congress in 2017: <br><br>“Combating domestic terrorism? Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |

Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |

Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |
| [T0068 Respond to Breaking News Event or Active Crisis](../../generated_pages/techniques/T0068.md) | <i>Social media users have been sharing images online that attribute various quotes to Speaker of the House Nancy Pelosi, Democratic presidential candidate Joe Biden and Rep. Alexandria Ocasio-Cortez. Reuters could not find evidence that these any of these quotes are accurate (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution).<br><br>[...]<br><br>The image reads: “’You need to vote for the Democrats, otherwise the illegal aliens will lose their rights.’ – Nancy Pelosi (2019), ‘No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights.’ – Joe Biden, And my personal favorite: ‘Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the Constitution.’ – Alexandria Ocasio Cortez (2018)”<br><br>The image doesn’t say where or when any of the alleged comments were made.<br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters could not find any records of Speaker Pelosi saying “’You need to vote for the Democrats, otherwise the illegal aliens will lose their rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)”<br><br>A Google search brings up pages using this quote with no attribution to a source.<br><br>In a press conference in June 2018, Pelosi told a reporter that using terminology like “illegal alien” is not constructive. The video is available on C-SPAN. Her exact words can be heard around the 15:30 mark. It is therefore unlikely that Pelosi would have used the terminology in the alleged quote. <br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters found no evidence former Vice President Biden ever said the words “No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)” <br><br>Some forums and posts featuring the article link to a Breitbart article that reads, “Biden: No Ordinary American Cares About Their Constitutional Rights, Facebook Questions are Plants”. The article mentions a February 21, 2013 forum at Western Connecticut State University in Danbury where then Vice President Biden spoke about gun control.<br><br>A video on the New York Times website shows Biden’s speech at the university. The closest to the quote in the claim can be seen round the 11:10 mark: “No law-abiding citizen in the United States of America has any fear that their constitutional rights will be infringed in any way. None, zero.”<br><br>The actual quote is significantly different to the quote in this claim. Biden did not say “No ordinary American cares about their constitutional rights”. (T0162: Reframe Context, T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)<br><br>[...]<br><br>“Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the constitution.”<br><br>Reuters could not find any record of Ocasio-Cortez saying this. The social media posts do not provide any context or other information about the purported quote (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution). <br><br>Ocasio-Cortez clarified her stance on the second amendment on the right to keep and bear arms while answering questions on a Reddit thread when she was running as a candidate for Congress in 2017: <br><br>“Combating domestic terrorism? Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |

(T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)”<br><br>A Google search brings up pages using this quote with no attribution to a source.<br><br>In a press conference in June 2018, Pelosi told a reporter that using terminology like “illegal alien” is not constructive. The video is available on C-SPAN. Her exact words can be heard around the 15:30 mark. It is therefore unlikely that Pelosi would have used the terminology in the alleged quote. <br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters found no evidence former Vice President Biden ever said the words “No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)” <br><br>Some forums and posts featuring the article link to a Breitbart article that reads, “Biden: No Ordinary American Cares About Their Constitutional Rights, Facebook Questions are Plants”. The article mentions a February 21, 2013 forum at Western Connecticut State University in Danbury where then Vice President Biden spoke about gun control.<br><br>A video on the New York Times website shows Biden’s speech at the university. The closest to the quote in the claim can be seen round the 11:10 mark: “No law-abiding citizen in the United States of America has any fear that their constitutional rights will be infringed in any way. None, zero.”<br><br>The actual quote is significantly different to the quote in this claim. Biden did not say “No ordinary American cares about their constitutional rights”. (T0162: Reframe Context, T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)<br><br>[...]<br><br>“Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the constitution.”<br><br>Reuters could not find any record of Ocasio-Cortez saying this. The social media posts do not provide any context or other information about the purported quote (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution). <br><br>Ocasio-Cortez clarified her stance on the second amendment on the right to keep and bear arms while answering questions on a Reddit thread when she was running as a candidate for Congress in 2017: <br><br>“Combating domestic terrorism? Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |

If it were a right, it would be in the constitution.”<br><br>Reuters could not find any record of Ocasio-Cortez saying this. Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |

If it were a right, it would be in the Constitution.’ – Alexandria Ocasio Cortez (2018)”<br><br>The image doesn’t say where or when any of the alleged comments were made.<br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters could not find any records of Speaker Pelosi saying “’You need to vote for the Democrats, otherwise the illegal aliens will lose their rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)”<br><br>A Google search brings up pages using this quote with no attribution to a source.<br><br>In a press conference in June 2018, Pelosi told a reporter that using terminology like “illegal alien” is not constructive. The video is available on C-SPAN. Her exact words can be heard around the 15:30 mark. It is therefore unlikely that Pelosi would have used the terminology in the alleged quote. <br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters found no evidence former Vice President Biden ever said the words “No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)” <br><br>Some forums and posts featuring the article link to a Breitbart article that reads, “Biden: No Ordinary American Cares About Their Constitutional Rights, Facebook Questions are Plants”. The article mentions a February 21, 2013 forum at Western Connecticut State University in Danbury where then Vice President Biden spoke about gun control.<br><br>A video on the New York Times website shows Biden’s speech at the university. The closest to the quote in the claim can be seen round the 11:10 mark: “No law-abiding citizen in the United States of America has any fear that their constitutional rights will be infringed in any way. None, zero.”<br><br>The actual quote is significantly different to the quote in this claim. Biden did not say “No ordinary American cares about their constitutional rights”. (T0162: Reframe Context, T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)<br><br>[...]<br><br>“Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the constitution.”<br><br>Reuters could not find any record of Ocasio-Cortez saying this. The social media posts do not provide any context or other information about the purported quote (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution). <br><br>Ocasio-Cortez clarified her stance on the second amendment on the right to keep and bear arms while answering questions on a Reddit thread when she was running as a candidate for Congress in 2017: <br><br>“Combating domestic terrorism? Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |

If it were a right, it would be in the constitution.”<br><br>Reuters could not find any record of Ocasio-Cortez saying this. Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. If it were a right, it would be in the Constitution.’ – Alexandria Ocasio Cortez (2018)”<br><br>The image doesn’t say where or when any of the alleged comments were made.<br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters could not find any records of Speaker Pelosi saying “’You need to vote for the Democrats, otherwise the illegal aliens will lose their rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)”<br><br>A Google search brings up pages using this quote with no attribution to a source.<br><br>In a press conference in June 2018, Pelosi told a reporter that using terminology like “illegal alien” is not constructive. The video is available on C-SPAN. Her exact words can be heard around the 15:30 mark. It is therefore unlikely that Pelosi would have used the terminology in the alleged quote. <br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters found no evidence former Vice President Biden ever said the words “No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)” <br><br>Some forums and posts featuring the article link to a Breitbart article that reads, “Biden: No Ordinary American Cares About Their Constitutional Rights, Facebook Questions are Plants”. The article mentions a February 21, 2013 forum at Western Connecticut State University in Danbury where then Vice President Biden spoke about gun control.<br><br>A video on the New York Times website shows Biden’s speech at the university. The closest to the quote in the claim can be seen round the 11:10 mark: “No law-abiding citizen in the United States of America has any fear that their constitutional rights will be infringed in any way. None, zero.”<br><br>The actual quote is significantly different to the quote in this claim. Biden did not say “No ordinary American cares about their constitutional rights”. (T0162: Reframe Context, T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)<br><br>[...]<br><br>“Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the constitution.”<br><br>Reuters could not find any record of Ocasio-Cortez saying this. The social media posts do not provide any context or other information about the purported quote (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution). <br><br>Ocasio-Cortez clarified her stance on the second amendment on the right to keep and bear arms while answering questions on a Reddit thread when she was running as a candidate for Congress in 2017: <br><br>“Combating domestic terrorism? Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |

If it were a right, it would be in the constitution.”<br><br>Reuters could not find any record of Ocasio-Cortez saying this. Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. If it were a right, it would be in the Constitution.’ – Alexandria Ocasio Cortez (2018)”<br><br>The image doesn’t say where or when any of the alleged comments were made.<br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters could not find any records of Speaker Pelosi saying “’You need to vote for the Democrats, otherwise the illegal aliens will lose their rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)”<br><br>A Google search brings up pages using this quote with no attribution to a source.<br><br>In a press conference in June 2018, Pelosi told a reporter that using terminology like “illegal alien” is not constructive. The video is available on C-SPAN. Her exact words can be heard around the 15:30 mark. It is therefore unlikely that Pelosi would have used the terminology in the alleged quote. <br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters found no evidence former Vice President Biden ever said the words “No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)” <br><br>Some forums and posts featuring the article link to a Breitbart article that reads, “Biden: No Ordinary American Cares About Their Constitutional Rights, Facebook Questions are Plants”. The article mentions a February 21, 2013 forum at Western Connecticut State University in Danbury where then Vice President Biden spoke about gun control.<br><br>A video on the New York Times website shows Biden’s speech at the university. The closest to the quote in the claim can be seen round the 11:10 mark: “No law-abiding citizen in the United States of America has any fear that their constitutional rights will be infringed in any way. None, zero.”<br><br>The actual quote is significantly different to the quote in this claim. Biden did not say “No ordinary American cares about their constitutional rights”. (T0162: Reframe Context, T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)<br><br>[...]<br><br>“Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the constitution.”<br><br>Reuters could not find any record of Ocasio-Cortez saying this. The social media posts do not provide any context or other information about the purported quote (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution). <br><br>Ocasio-Cortez clarified her stance on the second amendment on the right to keep and bear arms while answering questions on a Reddit thread when she was running as a candidate for Congress in 2017: <br><br>“Combating domestic terrorism? Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |

None, zero.”<br><br>The actual quote is significantly different to the quote in this claim. Biden did not say “No ordinary American cares about their constitutional rights”. (T0162: Reframe Context, T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)<br><br>[...]<br><br>“Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the constitution.”<br><br>Reuters could not find any record of Ocasio-Cortez saying this. The social media posts do not provide any context or other information about the purported quote (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution). <br><br>Ocasio-Cortez clarified her stance on the second amendment on the right to keep and bear arms while answering questions on a Reddit thread when she was running as a candidate for Congress in 2017: <br><br>“Combating domestic terrorism? Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |

Reuters could not find evidence that these any of these quotes are accurate (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution).<br><br>[...]<br><br>The image reads: “’You need to vote for the Democrats, otherwise the illegal aliens will lose their rights.’ – Nancy Pelosi (2019), ‘No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights.’ – Joe Biden, And my personal favorite: ‘Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the Constitution.’ – Alexandria Ocasio Cortez (2018)”<br><br>The image doesn’t say where or when any of the alleged comments were made.<br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters could not find any records of Speaker Pelosi saying “’You need to vote for the Democrats, otherwise the illegal aliens will lose their rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)”<br><br>A Google search brings up pages using this quote with no attribution to a source.<br><br>In a press conference in June 2018, Pelosi told a reporter that using terminology like “illegal alien” is not constructive. The video is available on C-SPAN. Her exact words can be heard around the 15:30 mark. It is therefore unlikely that Pelosi would have used the terminology in the alleged quote. <br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters found no evidence former Vice President Biden ever said the words “No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)” <br><br>Some forums and posts featuring the article link to a Breitbart article that reads, “Biden: No Ordinary American Cares About Their Constitutional Rights, Facebook Questions are Plants”. The article mentions a February 21, 2013 forum at Western Connecticut State University in Danbury where then Vice President Biden spoke about gun control.<br><br>A video on the New York Times website shows Biden’s speech at the university. The closest to the quote in the claim can be seen round the 11:10 mark: “No law-abiding citizen in the United States of America has any fear that their constitutional rights will be infringed in any way. None, zero.”<br><br>The actual quote is significantly different to the quote in this claim. Biden did not say “No ordinary American cares about their constitutional rights”. (T0162: Reframe Context, T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)<br><br>[...]<br><br>“Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the constitution.”<br><br>Reuters could not find any record of Ocasio-Cortez saying this. The social media posts do not provide any context or other information about the purported quote (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution). <br><br>Ocasio-Cortez clarified her stance on the second amendment on the right to keep and bear arms while answering questions on a Reddit thread when she was running as a candidate for Congress in 2017: <br><br>“Combating domestic terrorism? Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |
| [T0162.001 Incorrect Subtitled Speech Reframes Context](../../generated_pages/techniques/T0162.001.md) | <i>Social media users have been sharing images online that attribute various quotes to Speaker of the House Nancy Pelosi, Democratic presidential candidate Joe Biden and Rep. Alexandria Ocasio-Cortez. Reuters could not find evidence that these any of these quotes are accurate (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution).<br><br>[...]<br><br>The image reads: “’You need to vote for the Democrats, otherwise the illegal aliens will lose their rights.’ – Nancy Pelosi (2019), ‘No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights.’ – Joe Biden, And my personal favorite: ‘Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the Constitution.’ – Alexandria Ocasio Cortez (2018)”<br><br>The image doesn’t say where or when any of the alleged comments were made.<br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters could not find any records of Speaker Pelosi saying “’You need to vote for the Democrats, otherwise the illegal aliens will lose their rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)”<br><br>A Google search brings up pages using this quote with no attribution to a source.<br><br>In a press conference in June 2018, Pelosi told a reporter that using terminology like “illegal alien” is not constructive. The video is available on C-SPAN. Her exact words can be heard around the 15:30 mark. It is therefore unlikely that Pelosi would have used the terminology in the alleged quote. <br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters found no evidence former Vice President Biden ever said the words “No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)” <br><br>Some forums and posts featuring the article link to a Breitbart article that reads, “Biden: No Ordinary American Cares About Their Constitutional Rights, Facebook Questions are Plants”. The article mentions a February 21, 2013 forum at Western Connecticut State University in Danbury where then Vice President Biden spoke about gun control.<br><br>A video on the New York Times website shows Biden’s speech at the university. The closest to the quote in the claim can be seen round the 11:10 mark: “No law-abiding citizen in the United States of America has any fear that their constitutional rights will be infringed in any way. None, zero.”<br><br>The actual quote is significantly different to the quote in this claim. Biden did not say “No ordinary American cares about their constitutional rights”. (T0162: Reframe Context, T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)<br><br>[...]<br><br>“Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the constitution.”<br><br>Reuters could not find any record of Ocasio-Cortez saying this. The social media posts do not provide any context or other information about the purported quote (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution). <br><br>Ocasio-Cortez clarified her stance on the second amendment on the right to keep and bear arms while answering questions on a Reddit thread when she was running as a candidate for Congress in 2017: <br><br>“Combating domestic terrorism? Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |
| [T0162.002 Edits Made to News Report which Reframe Context](../../generated_pages/techniques/T0162.002.md) | <i>Social media users have been sharing images online that attribute various quotes to Speaker of the House Nancy Pelosi, Democratic presidential candidate Joe Biden and Rep. Alexandria Ocasio-Cortez. Reuters could not find evidence that these any of these quotes are accurate (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution).<br><br>[...]<br><br>The image reads: “’You need to vote for the Democrats, otherwise the illegal aliens will lose their rights.’ – Nancy Pelosi (2019), ‘No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights.’ – Joe Biden, And my personal favorite: ‘Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the Constitution.’ – Alexandria Ocasio Cortez (2018)”<br><br>The image doesn’t say where or when any of the alleged comments were made.<br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters could not find any records of Speaker Pelosi saying “’You need to vote for the Democrats, otherwise the illegal aliens will lose their rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)”<br><br>A Google search brings up pages using this quote with no attribution to a source.<br><br>In a press conference in June 2018, Pelosi told a reporter that using terminology like “illegal alien” is not constructive. The video is available on C-SPAN. Her exact words can be heard around the 15:30 mark. It is therefore unlikely that Pelosi would have used the terminology in the alleged quote. <br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters found no evidence former Vice President Biden ever said the words “No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)” <br><br>Some forums and posts featuring the article link to a Breitbart article that reads, “Biden: No Ordinary American Cares About Their Constitutional Rights, Facebook Questions are Plants”. The closest to the quote in the claim can be seen round the 11:10 mark: “No law-abiding citizen in the United States of America has any fear that their constitutional rights will be infringed in any way. If it were a right, it would be in the constitution.”<br><br>Reuters could not find any record of Ocasio-Cortez saying this. The social media posts do not provide any context or other information about the purported quote (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution). <br><br>Ocasio-Cortez clarified her stance on the second amendment on the right to keep and bear arms while answering questions on a Reddit thread when she was running as a candidate for Congress in 2017: <br><br>“Combating domestic terrorism? Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |

The closest to the quote in the claim can be seen round the 11:10 mark: “No law-abiding citizen in the United States of America has any fear that their constitutional rights will be infringed in any way. None, zero.”<br><br>The actual quote is significantly different to the quote in this claim. Biden did not say “No ordinary American cares about their constitutional rights”. (T0162: Reframe Context, T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)<br><br>[...]<br><br>“Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the constitution.”<br><br>Reuters could not find any record of Ocasio-Cortez saying this. The social media posts do not provide any context or other information about the purported quote (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution). <br><br>Ocasio-Cortez clarified her stance on the second amendment on the right to keep and bear arms while answering questions on a Reddit thread when she was running as a candidate for Congress in 2017: <br><br>“Combating domestic terrorism? Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |

I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |

(T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)”<br><br>A Google search brings up pages using this quote with no attribution to a source.<br><br>In a press conference in June 2018, Pelosi told a reporter that using terminology like “illegal alien” is not constructive. The video is available on C-SPAN. Her exact words can be heard around the 15:30 mark. It is therefore unlikely that Pelosi would have used the terminology in the alleged quote. <br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters found no evidence former Vice President Biden ever said the words “No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)” <br><br>Some forums and posts featuring the article link to a Breitbart article that reads, “Biden: No Ordinary American Cares About Their Constitutional Rights, Facebook Questions are Plants”. The article mentions a February 21, 2013 forum at Western Connecticut State University in Danbury where then Vice President Biden spoke about gun control.<br><br>A video on the New York Times website shows Biden’s speech at the university. The closest to the quote in the claim can be seen round the 11:10 mark: “No law-abiding citizen in the United States of America has any fear that their constitutional rights will be infringed in any way. None, zero.”<br><br>The actual quote is significantly different to the quote in this claim. Biden did not say “No ordinary American cares about their constitutional rights”. (T0162: Reframe Context, T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)<br><br>[...]<br><br>“Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the constitution.”<br><br>Reuters could not find any record of Ocasio-Cortez saying this. The social media posts do not provide any context or other information about the purported quote (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution). <br><br>Ocasio-Cortez clarified her stance on the second amendment on the right to keep and bear arms while answering questions on a Reddit thread when she was running as a candidate for Congress in 2017: <br><br>“Combating domestic terrorism? Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |

(T0162: Reframe Context, T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)<br><br>[...]<br><br>“Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the constitution.”<br><br>Reuters could not find any record of Ocasio-Cortez saying this. The social media posts do not provide any context or other information about the purported quote (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution). <br><br>Ocasio-Cortez clarified her stance on the second amendment on the right to keep and bear arms while answering questions on a Reddit thread when she was running as a candidate for Congress in 2017: <br><br>“Combating domestic terrorism? Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |

If it were a right, it would be in the Constitution.’ – Alexandria Ocasio Cortez (2018)”<br><br>The image doesn’t say where or when any of the alleged comments were made.<br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters could not find any records of Speaker Pelosi saying “’You need to vote for the Democrats, otherwise the illegal aliens will lose their rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)”<br><br>A Google search brings up pages using this quote with no attribution to a source.<br><br>In a press conference in June 2018, Pelosi told a reporter that using terminology like “illegal alien” is not constructive. The video is available on C-SPAN. Her exact words can be heard around the 15:30 mark. It is therefore unlikely that Pelosi would have used the terminology in the alleged quote. <br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters found no evidence former Vice President Biden ever said the words “No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)” <br><br>Some forums and posts featuring the article link to a Breitbart article that reads, “Biden: No Ordinary American Cares About Their Constitutional Rights, Facebook Questions are Plants”. The article mentions a February 21, 2013 forum at Western Connecticut State University in Danbury where then Vice President Biden spoke about gun control.<br><br>A video on the New York Times website shows Biden’s speech at the university. The closest to the quote in the claim can be seen round the 11:10 mark: “No law-abiding citizen in the United States of America has any fear that their constitutional rights will be infringed in any way. None, zero.”<br><br>The actual quote is significantly different to the quote in this claim. Biden did not say “No ordinary American cares about their constitutional rights”. (T0162: Reframe Context, T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)<br><br>[...]<br><br>“Owning guns is not a right. Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |

If it were a right, it would be in the constitution.”<br><br>Reuters could not find any record of Ocasio-Cortez saying this. The social media posts do not provide any context or other information about the purported quote (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution). <br><br>Ocasio-Cortez clarified her stance on the second amendment on the right to keep and bear arms while answering questions on a Reddit thread when she was running as a candidate for Congress in 2017: <br><br>“Combating domestic terrorism? Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |
| [T0167.001 Use of Clickbait](../../generated_pages/techniques/T0167.001.md) | <i>Social media users have been sharing images online that attribute various quotes to Speaker of the House Nancy Pelosi, Democratic presidential candidate Joe Biden and Rep. Alexandria Ocasio-Cortez. Reuters could not find evidence that these any of these quotes are accurate (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution).<br><br>[...]<br><br>The image reads: “’You need to vote for the Democrats, otherwise the illegal aliens will lose their rights.’ – Nancy Pelosi (2019), ‘No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights.’ – Joe Biden, And my personal favorite: ‘Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the Constitution.’ – Alexandria Ocasio Cortez (2018)”<br><br>The image doesn’t say where or when any of the alleged comments were made.<br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters could not find any records of Speaker Pelosi saying “’You need to vote for the Democrats, otherwise the illegal aliens will lose their rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)”<br><br>A Google search brings up pages using this quote with no attribution to a source.<br><br>In a press conference in June 2018, Pelosi told a reporter that using terminology like “illegal alien” is not constructive. The video is available on C-SPAN. Her exact words can be heard around the 15:30 mark. It is therefore unlikely that Pelosi would have used the terminology in the alleged quote. <br><br>[...]<br><br>Reuters found no evidence former Vice President Biden ever said the words “No ordinary American cares about Constitutional rights. (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)” <br><br>Some forums and posts featuring the article link to a Breitbart article that reads, “Biden: No Ordinary American Cares About Their Constitutional Rights, Facebook Questions are Plants”. The article mentions a February 21, 2013 forum at Western Connecticut State University in Danbury where then Vice President Biden spoke about gun control.<br><br>A video on the New York Times website shows Biden’s speech at the university. The closest to the quote in the claim can be seen round the 11:10 mark: “No law-abiding citizen in the United States of America has any fear that their constitutional rights will be infringed in any way. None, zero.”<br><br>The actual quote is significantly different to the quote in this claim. Biden did not say “No ordinary American cares about their constitutional rights”. (T0162: Reframe Context, T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution)<br><br>[...]<br><br>“Owning guns is not a right. If it were a right, it would be in the constitution.”<br><br>Reuters could not find any record of Ocasio-Cortez saying this. The social media posts do not provide any context or other information about the purported quote (T0161.002: Statement Incorrectly Presented as Made by Individual or Institution). <br><br>Ocasio-Cortez clarified her stance on the second amendment on the right to keep and bear arms while answering questions on a Reddit thread when she was running as a candidate for Congress in 2017: <br><br>“Combating domestic terrorism? Keep the severely mentally ill and people with a history of domestic abuse from purchasing guns. I am a believer in the second amendment, but this is where I draw the line.”<br><br>On her website, she calls for “common sense gun reform with the goal of eliminating gun violence and saving lives”<br><br>It is unlikely that, as a Congresswoman, Ocasio-Cortez would not be aware of the existence and meaning of the second amendment.<br><br>Reuters previously debunked the Biden and Ocasio-Cortez quotes (T0160.007: Claim Previously Fact Checked), along with other false quotes attributed to prominent Democrats.</i> |
